    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

<span id="freeTextContainer9776584585995257681">I'm going to start off by saying that I love Movie Companion books. I love looking behind the movie to see how they're made, how they're casted, and any other lit tidbit I can soak up. This one was no different. I loved <i>Divergent</i> and was actually impressed with the movie. What I liked about the companion was that it explained the transfer from book to screen from a visual aspect. Veronica Roth herself has said that she's not a very descriptive person and that was lacking in <i>Divergent</i>. The compan</span>
  <span id="freeText9776584585995257681" style="display:none">I'm going to start off by saying that I love Movie Companion books. I love looking behind the movie to see how they're made, how they're casted, and any other lit tidbit I can soak up. This one was no different. I loved <i>Divergent</i> and was actually impressed with the movie. What I liked about the companion was that it explained the transfer from book to screen from a visual aspect. Veronica Roth herself has said that she's not a very descriptive person and that was lacking in <i>Divergent</i>. The companion talked a lot about how the director created the world with little to go on but tried to stay true to what Roth had already created - especially concerning costumes and living quarters. I'm always fascinated by the process of film making so I revel in anything that can further my obsession and these companions do exactly that. </span>

The pictures used are fantastic and side in with the information provided well.   <span id="freeText15966079929876640218" style="display:none">I loved this. It examined every inch of the book to movie journey, and I savoured every moment. The pictures used are fantastic and side in with the information provided well. What I found most interesting was the fact that they picked out Shailenne Woodley for the part of Tris in a quick fashion, yet Tobias was one of the last characters casted (by the oh-so-handsome Theo James). I bought this before I went to see the movie and looked out for Veronica Roth's little screen time, which was insanely cool. She stared in her own idea (look out for her in the zip line scene, she is where Uriah would be if he actually got casted -_-)! All in all, would definetely recommend this title to any die hard Divergent fans (like myself!) or just anyone purely interested in the behind the scenes work of the movie. Fantastic read. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12009198908423628239"><p>An amazing guide of how book-to-movie adaptaions are made, specifically Divergent. I'm a big fan of Divergent series and ofc of Veronica Roth, so I was genuinely astonished to find out how much filmmakers where in love with the book and that their cared for story as much as fans were. It really shows that there're still people out there who care about how stories are made and not just greedy for money. The amount of involvement of Veronica Roth in process just warmed my heart. Like everytime you</p></span>
  <span id="freeText12009198908423628239" style="display:none"><p>An amazing guide of how book-to-movie adaptaions are made, specifically Divergent. I'm a big fan of Divergent series and ofc of Veronica Roth, so I was genuinely astonished to find out how much filmmakers where in love with the book and that their cared for story as much as fans were. It really shows that there're still people out there who care about how stories are made and not just greedy for money. The amount of involvement of Veronica Roth in process just warmed my heart. Like everytime you see her radiating smile in a picture with cast members or filmmakers, it's just makes you smile too.</p><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"The aptitude test and the Choosing Ceremony exclude and deny Divergents. But it’s in her Divergence, finally, that Tris finds her greatest strength. When she embraces the full range of her qualities as a human being, she can play an active role in her world. Even as it is falling apart."</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><p>Looking at pictures of Shailene and Theo as their characters is breathtaking. They both look spectacular and authentic. The chemestry between them in the movies is insane and mind-blowing. Love them soooo much!!!</p><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1571486531ra/28319370.gif" width="320" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><p>I've never thought that filmmaking process could be so painstaking and detailed. It really did change my perception of how movies are made in general. Definitely worth reading!</p></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wise Cat" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wise Cat" href="/user/show/14678435-wise-cat">Wise Cat</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780062315625" href="/book/show/18498577-divergent-official-illustrated-movie-companion">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Anyone who loved the movie and/or book</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Wise Cat by: </span>
      No one
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14678435-wise-cat?shelf=non-fiction">non-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14678435-wise-cat?shelf=dystopian-ya">dystopian-ya</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1091382172" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4874684890115429920">I really ought to read companion books about a movie more often. I didn't think of doing this, until this came up with the Divergent books in the library database.<br/><br/>Enjoyed this immensely, esp. all the backstory of how they did the casting, how they shot certain scenes, which actors did their own stunts, where it was filmed, how the locals responded to the shooting in Chicago, etc.<br/><br/>Only wish there was more detail on how it was like for Winslet to work with the younger (up and coming in talent)cast.</span>
  <span id="freeText4874684890115429920" style="display:none">I really ought to read companion books about a movie more often. I didn't think of doing this, until this came up with the Divergent books in the library database.<br /><br />Enjoyed this immensely, esp. all the backstory of how they did the casting, how they shot certain scenes, which actors did their own stunts, where it was filmed, how the locals responded to the shooting in Chicago, etc.<br /><br />Only wish there was more detail on how it was like for Winslet to work with the younger (up and coming in talent)cast. I didn't know Kate was 5 months pregnant at the time, so she wasn't going to be around much for shooting as much as the others. I found it interesting how she saw herself in a young Shailene Woodley, when she herself was a promising, young actress.<br /><br />Woodley sounds as fearless as her character. I wasn't aware she did some of her own stunts when possible, nor that she had a double for some scenes. I figured she must have though!<br /><br />I loved the photos in this book as well, and I thought Theo James as Four was perfect. I didn't picture Peter as Miles Teller, but he/is good in the role. Great that the cast got to be friendly off screen as well as on, such as between Christina/Tris (or Zoe/Shailene).<br /><br />I was fascinated on how much effort went into the costumes as well. The books don't describe in much detail on what each faction wore, so it was up to the wardrobe department to imagine what they wore. Didn't know Roth herself appeared as an extra, as one of the Dauntless. Guess I didn't expect that, so I didn't even look for her. Also, I've only seen her picture a couple of times, so her face didn't register well.<br /><br />The insight from the cast and crew on the story/characters was my favorite part, along with all those beautiful pictures.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4874684890115429920" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer909121337" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13320766922257574868">I have both of the Hunger Games movie companion books (The Hunger Games and The Hunger Games: Catching Fire) and I really enjoyed both. When I saw that this one was written by the same author I decided to pick it up, thinking that it would be written in the same style as the other two. I wasn’t disappointed. <br/><br/>Actually, that’s not totally true. I waited to pick them up until I was sure that the movie wasn’t awful (it was really good – go see it if you haven’t yet). <br/><br/>This book is very similar to the</span>
  <span id="freeText13320766922257574868" style="display:none">I have both of the Hunger Games movie companion books (The Hunger Games and The Hunger Games: Catching Fire) and I really enjoyed both. When I saw that this one was written by the same author I decided to pick it up, thinking that it would be written in the same style as the other two. I wasn’t disappointed. <br /><br />Actually, that’s not totally true. I waited to pick them up until I was sure that the movie wasn’t awful (it was really good – go see it if you haven’t yet). <br /><br />This book is very similar to the two Hunger Games illustrated movie companions. The books are just beautiful: filled with lots of photographs, both of movie stills and behind the scenes moments. Author Kate Egan spoke with many of the people involved in the movie (the director and many of the actors, among others) and the book is filled with quotes from them. <br /><br />There’s even a short section devoted to Kate Winslet!<br /><br />The book has a pretty large trim size, again equal to the two Hunger Games movie companion books. This is a great format for all of the photos. <br /><br />If you are a fan of the movie, I would say to definitely get this one. <br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6245490585602137628">I am completely awe-struck.<br/>To be completely honest with you, Divergent is one of my favorite books of all time so I must say that I was very skeptical with the movie. I noticed and criticized things that most people didn't see. <br/>But, wow. The level of fascination reading this was very high. Seeing how it all came together.   <span id="freeText6245490585602137628" style="display:none">I am completely awe-struck.<br />To be completely honest with you, Divergent is one of my favorite books of all time so I must say that I was very skeptical with the movie. I noticed and criticized things that most people didn't see. <br />But, wow. The level of fascination reading this was very high. Seeing how it all came together. What every single location or moment meant to the movie was utterly incredible. The amount of thought that was put into this movie blew me away.<br />I have always been interested in film-making, I wish to study something that is related to it in the future (which might be impossible where I live) however, seeing how everything come together is truly exhilarating.<br /><br />From how screenplays are written, to the visual effects of the scenes. A whole world being built.<br />Also, I absolutely loved taking an insight picture of how Divergent was written in the first place.<br /><br />For any fan of Divergent, whether you like the movie or the book this is definitely a must!</span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25678046-robin?shelf=_read-in-2014">_read-in-2014</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<span id="freeTextContainer5314744642621931447">This book is pretty standard for a "movie companion" book - it contains details on book to script transition, casting the roles, the cast & crew, how the sets and costumes were designed, and aspects of shooting the movie itself.<br/><br/>The costume design sketches for all the factions were well done, and I feel they really represented the ideals of the factions.<br/>I liked how they discussed the accent colors of the Dauntless outfits, that was something I hadn't noticed in the movie.<br/><br/>I found the details of th</span>
  <span id="freeText5314744642621931447" style="display:none">This book is pretty standard for a "movie companion" book - it contains details on book to script transition, casting the roles, the cast &amp; crew, how the sets and costumes were designed, and aspects of shooting the movie itself.<br /><br />The costume design sketches for all the factions were well done, and I feel they really represented the ideals of the factions.<br />I liked how they discussed the accent colors of the Dauntless outfits, that was something I hadn't noticed in the movie.<br /><br />I found the details of the set design &amp; location to be the most interesting part of the book. I enjoyed reading how the Abnegation Village location was created. I would have liked to read more about how the Dauntless HQ was laid out and designed.<br /><br />Overall, it was an good read.</span>

<div id="review_983834587" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/983834587" />
    <a title="Justine" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4818199-justine"><img alt="Justine" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442180952p2/4818199.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/983834587?book_show_action=true">Jul 02, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Justine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Justine" href="/user/show/4818199-justine">Justine</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer983834587" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10605114375085271056">I'm really interested in reading movie companions because I haven't read too many. I wasn't sure what to expect with this one. I really liked it because it covered everything: the plot/ story, characters, actors and even some behind the scenes. My favourite parts were of all of the costumes and makeup. I found this book to be very informative and I learned a lot about what goes into making a movie. Any Divergent fans need to add this book to their collection.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

I swear she sta</span>
  <span id="freeText38459521302546013" style="display:none"><b>DIVERGENT OFFICIAL ILLUSTRATED MOVIE COMPANION</b><br />(Movie Companion)<br />Kate Egan<br /><br /><b>[** ] 1 &amp; 1/2 Stars.</b><br /><br />Oh, hi there, Divergent Movie Picture Book!<br /><br /><br />There was a crapload of information here, not only on this movie in specific but also technicalities about how a movie is done. I loved, loved, loved this and it would get a higher rating if not for the author.<br /><br />Words from Veronica Roth, Neil Burger or anyone from the cast and crew were pretty much exciting but the rest was just dull and repetitive. I swear she started over half of her sencetences with "she/he remembered" and whatever they said. I don't mean to be rude or anything but is she five years old or something? From what little I know, you are required to have at least some writing skills to be an editor. This makes me sound like a bully. Let's paraphrase. I'm not saying that she doesn't have the skill, just that it doesn't show at all. I get that the basis of this book is Q&amp;As and pictures but still, I expected more. <br /><br /><br />Favorite Quotes: "Taken to extremes even the best human qualities would go sour." ― Veronica Roth. "[...] If you can dig deep inside yourself and power through, you just might be okay." ― Doug Wick.<br /><br /><br />-----<br />Song: Beating Heart by Ellie Goulding.</span>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/958361362?book_show_action=true">Jun 05, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Misty" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Misty" href="/user/show/3922547-misty">Misty</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780007555406" href="/book/show/21276870-the-divergent-official-illustrated-movie-companion">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3922547-misty?shelf=recieved-for-review">recieved-for-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3922547-misty?shelf=own">own</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer958361362" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6833404053956926423">The illustrated movie companion for the Divergent movie is full of beautiful images from the movie and behind the scenes. It also has some really interesting insight into what went into making the movie, like building the sets and even how much difficulty they had casting Four, I for one can say I'm glad they waited until the found the perfect actor because I couldn't imagine anyone other than Theo James playing him.<br/>I definitely think this book would make the perfect little extra for fans of the</span>
  <span id="freeText6833404053956926423" style="display:none">The illustrated movie companion for the Divergent movie is full of beautiful images from the movie and behind the scenes. It also has some really interesting insight into what went into making the movie, like building the sets and even how much difficulty they had casting Four, I for one can say I'm glad they waited until the found the perfect actor because I couldn't imagine anyone other than Theo James playing him.<br />I definitely think this book would make the perfect little extra for fans of the movie and/or books who want to know a little more of how making Divergent into a movie became a reality and its amazing to see just how dedicated the whole team were in being true to the book and the lengths they went to, to make sure the sets were perfect. It makes you realise that they didn't just make the movie for themselves but for the fans too whom they also used as extras in some scenes, something I didn't know.<br />So, if you're looking for something to tide you over while you're waiting for the DVD release so you can watch Divergent again, I 'd recommend picking this up, if for no more reason than there are full page pictures of Four in it!</span>
  <a data-text-id="6833404053956926423" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
